                 <h4 class="nspHeader tleft fnone has-image">
                  <a href="/kerrys-blog/2583-jade-helm-whistleblower-texas-emp" target="_self" title="JADE HELM WHISTLEBLOWER - TEXAS EMP?">
                   JADE HELM WHISTLEBLOWER - TEXAS EMP?
                  </a>
                 </h4>
                 <a class="nspImageWrapper tleft fleft" href="/kerrys-blog/2583-jade-helm-whistleblower-texas-emp" style="margin:0px 15px 0px 0px;" target="_self">
                  <img alt="JADE HELM WHISTLEBLOWER - TEXAS EMP?" class="nspImage tleft fleft" src="http://www.projectcamelotportal.com/modules/mod_news_pro_gk5/cache/WHITE_RABBIT_EMP_TEXAS2nsp-764.jpg" style="width:250px;height:250px;"/>
                 </a>
                 <p class="nspText tjustify fnull">
                  After publishing the interview with Dale Lewis, I was contacted by Dale who said that his friend who met the soldier who went AWOL was now willing to come forward and share his story.
This is the audio recording with the man who was approached in a convenience store in Texas, by the soldier. This man prefers to keep his name private and is using the moniker "White Rabbit".
I urge everyone to listen and carefully consider the possibility that a false flag attack may be about to occur in Texas. Regardless of what happens we believ...
